						&lt;br&gt;
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:20px; margin-right:20px; color:#000000; text-align: left; font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; height:170px&quot;&gt;
							&lt;br&gt;
							&lt;span style=&quot;margin-left:20px; font-size:25pt; line-height:1.5;&quot;&gt;Autonomous Database&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br&gt;
							&lt;span style=&quot;margin-left:20px; font-size:15pt; line-height:1.5;&quot;&gt;on Shared Exadata Infrastructure&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br&gt;
							&lt;span style=&quot;margin-left:20px; font-size:12pt; line-height:1.5;&quot;&gt;July 22, 2020&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
					
				
			
			&lt;a name=&quot;btt&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:20px;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;
						&lt;p&gt;Welcome to our latest customer newsletter for Autonomous Database on Shared Exadata Infrastructure.&amp;nbsp;This newsletter covers the following new features and topics:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;ul&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#gwno&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;Using Autonomous Data Guard&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#mdwp&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;MDW Patterns in OCI Resource Manager&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
						&lt;/ul&gt;

						&lt;p style=&quot;font-style: italic; font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size:14px; color:#000000;&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note:&lt;/strong&gt; some new features are only available with &lt;strong&gt;19c&lt;/strong&gt;. To get the most from Autonomous Database, upgrade to 19c as soon as possible. There is more information about how to upgrade existing 18c instances to 19c &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/autonomous-data-warehouse-cloud/user/autonomous-upgrade.html#GUID-47F4EA0B-C4B6-4135-A284-AE730D550F1C&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt; here, for ADW&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/atp-cloud/atpug/autonomous-upgrade.html#GUID-47F4EA0B-C4B6-4135-A284-AE730D550F1C&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;here, for ATP&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;Don&amp;#39;t forget to checkout our &lt;strong&gt;&amp;quot;What&amp;#39;s New&amp;quot;&lt;/strong&gt; page for a comprehensive archive of all the new features we have added to Autonomous Database - &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.oracle.com/database/technologies/datawarehouse-bigdata/adw-features.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;To find out how to subscribe to this newsletter &lt;a href=&quot;https://blogs.oracle.com/datawarehousing/announcing-customer-newsletter-for-autonomous-database&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			
			&lt;a name=&quot;gwno&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Icon for creating a standby dataabase&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/bb422732717be7b5766701bad5c22ac4/replication.png&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Creating a Standby Database with ADG&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;When you enable Autonomous Data Guard on ADB, the system creates a standby database that stays &amp;quot;connected&amp;quot; to the primary database and automatically refreshes its data from the primary database.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;This allows the following, depending on the state of the primary database:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot; style=&quot;margin-left:55px;&quot;&gt;If your primary database goes down, Autonomous Data Guard converts the standby database to the primary database with minimal interruption. After failover completes, Autonomous Data Guard automatically creates a new standby database.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot; style=&quot;margin-left:55px;&quot;&gt;You can perform a switchover operation, where the primary database becomes the standby database, and the standby database becomes the primary database.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note:&lt;/strong&gt; Autonomous Database does not provide access to the standby database.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;img alt=&quot;Simplified animated GIF showing creation of an Autonomous Data Guard standby instance for ADW&quot; id=&quot;myImg&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/3f425d604e4ec4fb55c3b40f8f72b98e/adg_animation.gif&quot; style=&quot;width:100%;max-width:550px&quot; /&gt; 
						&lt;div class=&quot;modal&quot; id=&quot;myModal&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;close&quot;&gt;&amp;times;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;img class=&quot;modal-content&quot; id=&quot;img01&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;div class=&quot;caption&quot; id=&quot;caption&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/div&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
// Get the modal
var modal = document.getElementById(&quot;myModal&quot;);

// Get the image and insert it inside the modal - use its &quot;alt&quot; text as a caption
var img = document.getElementById(&quot;myImg&quot;);
var modalImg = document.getElementById(&quot;img01&quot;);
var captionText = document.getElementById(&quot;caption&quot;);
img.onclick = function(){
  modal.style.display = &quot;block&quot;;
  modalImg.src = this.src;
  captionText.innerHTML = this.alt;
}

// Get the &lt;span&gt; element that closes the modal
var span = document.getElementsByClassName(&quot;close&quot;)[0];

// When the user clicks on &lt;span&gt; (x), close the modal
span.onclick = function() { 
  modal.style.display = &quot;none&quot;;
}

						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Using OCI Resource Manager to Deploy Data Warehouse Reference Architecture Patterns&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;The list of pre-built Stacks within OCI Resource Manager has been expanded to include some of the new reference architecture patterns. Currently, the Departmental Data Warehouse pattern is available as a pre-built stack and the other Modern Data Warehouse patterns will be available shortly.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;img alt=&quot;Simplified animated GIF showing automated deployment process for reference architecture patterns&quot; id=&quot;myImg02&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/82e90fd56d76658b232d34dbbae05799/rm_patterns.gif&quot; style=&quot;width:100%;max-width:550px&quot; /&gt; 
						&lt;div class=&quot;modal&quot; id=&quot;myModal02&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;close02&quot; id=&quot;close02&quot;&gt;&amp;times;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;img class=&quot;modal-content&quot; id=&quot;img02&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;div class=&quot;caption&quot; id=&quot;caption02&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/div&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;

						&amp;nbsp;
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:20px; margin-right:20px; color:#000000; text-align: left; font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; height:170px&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;margin-left:20px; font-size:25pt; line-height:1.5;&quot;&gt;Autonomous Database&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;margin-left:20px; font-size:15pt; line-height:1.5;&quot;&gt;on Shared Exadata Infrastructure&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;margin-left:20px; font-size:12pt; line-height:1.5;&quot;&gt;July 15, 2020&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
						
					
				
			
&lt;a name=&quot;btt&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:20px;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;
						&lt;p&gt;Welcome to our latest customer newsletter for Autonomous Database on Shared Exadata Infrastructure.&amp;nbsp;This newsletter covers the following new features and topics:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;ul&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#gwno&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;Connecting to non-Oracle Databases&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#mncs&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;Modify Network Configuration&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#tzfs&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;Timezone Support&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#mupp&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;Modifying User Profiles&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#gsgs&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;Updated Quick Start Guides&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#apex&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;APEX 20.1 is coming to ADB&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#dwgl&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;Global Leaders Update&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
						&lt;/ul&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;Don&amp;#39;t forget to checkout our &lt;strong&gt;&amp;quot;What&amp;#39;s New&amp;quot;&lt;/strong&gt; page for a comprehensive archive of all the new features we have added to Autonomous Database - &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.oracle.com/database/technologies/datawarehouse-bigdata/adw-features.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;To find out how to subscribe to this newsletter &lt;a href=&quot;https://blogs.oracle.com/datawarehousing/announcing-customer-newsletter-for-autonomous-database&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			
			&lt;a name=&quot;gwno&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Icon for ADB Connecting to non-Oracle Databases Using Gateways&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/5195072cc786ce37fa0dd61c219d885f/evolution_1of5.png&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Connecting to Non-Oracle Databases&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;Autonomous Database now supports using connections that are enabled via Oracle Database Gateway. Gateways are designed for accessing a specific non-Oracle Database such as DB2, Teradata, SQL Server etc.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;Oracle Database Gateway provide queries and applications with access to data anywhere in a distributed database system without knowing either the location of the data or how it is stored. This removes the need to customize applications to access data from non-Oracle systems.&lt;/p&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

						
							
								
									LEARN MORE

			&lt;a name=&quot;mncs&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Icon for ADB network settings&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/e84fe50993ddf49d462eee5d11219ba8/cloud_utilities_blue.png&quot; /&gt;

						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Modify Network Settings for ADB Instances&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;Autonomous Database now supports switching network access type. This feature enables customers to perform an in-place switch from public endpoint to private endpoint (and vice versa).&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						The feature will reduce customer effort required for switching between public and private endpoints and make it easier for customers to adopt private endpoint.&lt;/p&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

			&lt;a name=&quot;tzfs&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Icon for timezone files for autonomous database&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/ac4dd626a1f5421a914b1c8aaffd0440/clock_24_7_512.png&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Timezone Files Automatically Updated&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;For time zone support, Oracle Database uses time zone files that store the list of all time zones. The time zone files for Autonomous Database are periodically updated to reflect the latest time zone specific changes.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;An Autonomous Database instance will automatically pick up updated time zone files depending on the lifecycle state of the instance:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot; style=&quot;margin-left:45px;&quot;&gt;- Stopped: At the next start operation the update is automatically applied.&lt;br /&gt;
						- Available: After a restart the update is automatically applied.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;When a load or import operation results in a timezone related error, restart the ADB instance and try again.&lt;/p&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

						
							
								
									LEARN MORE

						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Icon for added security through user profiles and option to set password verification&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/4a4156c51124dac49aa37df2119cb9b2/security.png&quot; /&gt;

						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Create/Modify User Profile and Set Password Rules&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;Autonomous Database now supports the ability to create/alter user profiles and import existing user profiles from another environment with Oracle Data Pump Import.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;Cloud Admins can now manage the rules for password complexity on Autonomous Database. Administrators can can create a Password Verify Function (PVF) and associate the PVF with a profile to manage the rules for password complexity.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;UPDATE &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Quick Start Guides&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;new-window&quot; href=&quot;https://oracle.github.io/learning-library/data-management-library/autonomous-database/shared/adb-quickstart-workshop/freetier/&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Quickstart Tutorial 1: Autonomous Database Quickstart&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;new-window&quot; href=&quot;https://oracle.github.io/learning-library/data-management-library/autonomous-database/shared/adb-advanced-workshop/freetier/&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Quickstart Tutorial 2: Analyzing your data with Autonomous Database&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;Great news - &lt;strong&gt;Oracle APEX 20.1&lt;/strong&gt; is coming to Autonomous Database!&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						Always Free customers received the upgrade on July 8, 2020 and other customers will receive APEX 20.1 beginning July 17, 2020.&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						To receive the APEX 20.1 upgrade, customers must be on Oracle Database 19c. For more information about how to upgrade an existing ADB instance to 19c please follow the instructions in the documentation:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot; style=&quot;margin-left:55px;&quot;&gt;- &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/autonomous-data-warehouse-cloud/user/autonomous-upgrade.html#GUID-47F4EA0B-C4B6-4135-A284-AE730D550F1C&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;, for ADW&lt;br /&gt;
						- &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/atp-cloud/atpug/autonomous-upgrade.html#GUID-47F4EA0B-C4B6-4135-A284-AE730D550F1C&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt; click here&lt;/a&gt;, for ATP.&lt;/p&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Can I Validate My APEX Applications Before Upgrading?&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						Yes you can! There is a unique capability in APEX on Autonomous Database that enables customers to validate their applications prior to the APEX upgrade. Please see &lt;a href=&quot;https://blogs.oracle.com/apex/control-when-apex-is-upgraded-on-your-oracle-autonomous-database&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;this blog post&lt;/a&gt; for detailed instructions.&lt;/p&gt;

Cetin Ozbutun delivered the Executive Keynote on our Data Management Roadmap.&lt;/p&gt;

						&amp;nbsp;
						&lt;img alt=&quot;ADB Logo&quot; class=&quot;header_icon&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/3171ecca19062436f699f9aedcd05812/adb_header_icon_300.jpeg&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:20px;&quot; /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;

			&lt;a name=&quot;btt&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:20px;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;
						&lt;p&gt;Welcome to our latest customer newsletter for Autonomous Database on Shared Exadata Infrastructure.&amp;nbsp;This newsletter covers the following new features and topics:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;ul&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#orc&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;Support for ORC files&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#19c&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;Automatic upgrade to 19c&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#awr&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;AWR Reports in Performance Hub&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#ftl&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;Changes to file transfer limits into Object Store&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#ras&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;Procedures for using Database Real Application Security&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#rap&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot;&gt;Reference architecture patterns for data warehousing&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
						&lt;/ul&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;Don&amp;#39;t forget to checkout our &lt;strong&gt;&amp;quot;What&amp;#39;s New&amp;quot;&lt;/strong&gt; page for a comprehensive archive of all the new features we have added to Autonomous Database - &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.oracle.com/database/technologies/datawarehouse-bigdata/adw-features.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;To find out how to subscribe to this newsletter &lt;a href=&quot;https://blogs.oracle.com/datawarehousing/announcing-customer-newsletter-for-autonomous-database&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			
			&lt;a name=&quot;orc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;ADB Support for ORC files&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/7850eb5d39dcbb79b110d1deea442d81/apex_logo.jpg&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - ADB now supports ORC files&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;ADB has expanded object storage support in two important ways: it can now query &lt;a href=&quot;https://cwiki.apache.org/confluence/display/Hive/LanguageManual+ORC&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;ORC files&lt;/a&gt; as well as complex data types found in Parquet, ORC and Avro files.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p style=&quot;margin-left:25px; font-style:italic;&quot;&gt;The Optimized Row Columnar (ORC) file is a highly efficient way to store Hive data. It was designed to overcome limitations of the other Hive file formats. Like Parquet, ORC data is stored in a compressed columnar format and provides metadata to enable efficient reads.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;ORC, Parquet and Avro file types provide the ability to capture fields containing complex data types, including arrays, maps, unions and objects (or structs). These complex types can now be queried in ADB using Oracle&amp;rsquo;s extensive JSON query support.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;: support for ORC and complex data types are only available in 19c.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

						
							
								
									LEARN MORE
								
							
						

						
							
								
									
									&lt;div class=&quot;row_set&quot;&gt;
									&lt;p&gt;DOC: DBMS_CLOUD Package ORC to Oracle Data Type Mapping for ADW, &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/autonomous-data-warehouse-cloud/user/data-type-mapping-orc.html#GUID-A1699602-36F6-4C44-BAE6-48B7AFFA49F2&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;DOC: DBMS_CLOUD Package ORC, Parquet and Avro Complex Types for ADW, &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/autonomous-data-warehouse-cloud/user/complex-types-orc-avro-parquet.html#GUID-65E8035D-CCEF-4391-B4B4-745393A27412&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;DOC: DBMS_CLOUD Package ORC, Parquet and Avro Complex Types for ATP, &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/atp-cloud/atpug/complex-types-orc-avro-parquet.html#GUID-65E8035D-CCEF-4391-B4B4-745393A27412&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;DOC: DBMS_CLOUD Package ORC, Parquet and Avro to Oracle Column Name Mapping for ATP, &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/atp-cloud/atpug/avro-parquet-column-name.html#GUID-18DF63B6-C312-4FD3-9DED-8BFBE265C873&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
									&lt;/div&gt;

			&lt;a name=&quot;19c&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/7452caec8faf22b604482d875395e694/19c_logo.png&quot; /&gt;

						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NOTE&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Customer Announcement About Automatic Upgrade to 19c&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;An email announcement about the automatic upgrade to Database 19c has been sent to ADB customers (&lt;em&gt;see below&lt;/em&gt;). The automatic upgrade of Autonomous Databases will start in September.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;At the date of the scheduled upgrade, Autonomous Database instances will be automatically upgraded in-place to Oracle Database 19c.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;Please note that to better manage the customer experience during this upgrade process we are recommending that customers contact support by logging a service request if they have any questions about the upgrade process.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;img alt=&quot;Email message for Autonomous Database automatic upgrade to 19c&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/8667439a639aa900e4e4c19aa4d8a11a/upgrade_19c_550.png&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;To view the options for manually upgrading an exsting ADW instance to Database 19c - &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/autonomous-data-warehouse-cloud/user/autonomous-upgrade.html#GUID-47F4EA0B-C4B6-4135-A284-AE730D550F1C&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;To view the options for manually upgrading an exsting ATP instance to Database 19c - &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/atp-cloud/atpug/autonomous-upgrade.html#GUID-47F4EA0B-C4B6-4135-A284-AE730D550F1C&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

			&lt;a name=&quot;awr&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Icon for AWR Reports on Performance Hub&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/7262f9add7a1acfa96751223c00098ab/psb.png&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Download AWR Reports From Performance Hub&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;Automatic Workload Repository (AWR) report is a vital tool to collect historical performance statistics of an Oracle Database by DBAs and System Performance engineers.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;Performance Hub on the OCI console now allows customers to download an AWR report for a specific time period.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;img alt=&quot;AWR Reports now available via Performance Hub&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/7364d127a26bef2aef81d19bc431ddf9/awr_report_550.png&quot; /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;
						
							
								
									LEARN MORE
								
							
						

						
							
								
									
									&lt;div class=&quot;row_set&quot;&gt;
									&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;DOC: Using Performance Hub to Analyze Database Performance, &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.cloud.oracle.com/en-us/iaas/Content/Database/Tasks/perfhub.htm&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;DOC: Active Session History Reports, &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/database/oracle/oracle-database/19/tdppt/resolving-transient-performance-problems.html#GUID-7316A970-330C-4F1B-9F9A-7623EFE5B38C&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
									&lt;br /&gt;
									&amp;nbsp;&lt;/div&gt;
									
								
							
						
						&amp;nbsp;

						
							
								
									DO MORE
								
							
						

						
							
								
									
									&lt;div class=&quot;row_set&quot;&gt;
									&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;DOC: Interpreting Results from Active Session History Reports...&lt;br /&gt;
									After generating an ASH report, you can use the following sections to review its contents to help identify possible causes of transient performance problems:&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;ul&gt;
										&lt;li&gt;Top Events&lt;/li&gt;
										&lt;li&gt;Top SQL&lt;/li&gt;
										&lt;li&gt;Top PL/SQL&lt;/li&gt;
										&lt;li&gt;Top Sessions&lt;/li&gt;
										&lt;li&gt;Activity Over Time&lt;/li&gt;
									&lt;/ul&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/database/oracle/oracle-database/19/tgdba/analyzing-sampled-data.html#GUID-36ABAF67-227B-4CCA-9B44-F3A87244E7A3&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
									&lt;/div&gt;
									
								
							
						
						
						&amp;nbsp;

						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Icon for file size increaed when transferring files to OCI Object Store&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/d75f752a236eb0545a8f48d18f202313/gsm_logo1_3664622.png&quot; /&gt;

						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;UPDATE &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Maximum File Size Increased For Transfer Object Store&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;The maximum file size limit for DBMS_CLOUD.PUT_OBJECT procedure when transferring files to OCI Object Storage has been increased to 50 GB.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Note - there are different size restrictions when using other object stores such as Amazon S3 and Microsoft&amp;#39;s Azure Blob Storage. See doc links below for more details.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

									&lt;p&gt;DOC: Details of PUT_OBJECT procedure for ATP, &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/atp-cloud/atpug/dbms-cloud.html#GUID-716F0DE7-C669-477E-8AB8-EA42E41ACB12&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;UPDATE &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Reference Architecture Patterns and Solution Playbooks Now Available&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;The Architecture Center has been updated to include a new series of data warehouse patterns:&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;img alt=&quot;Reference Architecture Home Page&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/0282fc45399bb61c6d7d256508f6aa6a/rap_550.png&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;Each reference architecture pattern will come with the following: best practices framework; a set of recommendations which are a starting point for implementing the pattern and a terraform script for deploying the end-to-end set of cloud services on OCI.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;Currently, the following patterns are available (&lt;em&gt;note: more patterns are being built and will be added shortly&lt;/em&gt;):&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;ul&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/solutions/oci-ebs-analysis/index.html&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Departmental data warehousing - an EBS integration example&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/solutions/oci-spreadsheet-analysis/index.html&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Departmental data warehousing/data marts - consolidate spreadsheets&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/solutions/oci-curated-analysis/index.html&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Enterprise data warehousing - an integrated data lake example&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/solutions/data-science-environment/index.html#GUID-CE4B3020-881C-481D-B434-199388C3ADD3&quot; style=&quot;color: grey !important;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Set up a data science environment that uses Oracle Machine Learning&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;

						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			
			&lt;a name=&quot;btt&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:20px;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;
						&lt;p&gt;Welcome to our latest customer newsletter for Autonomous Database on Shared Exadata Infrastructure.&amp;nbsp;This newsletter covers the following new features and topics:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;ul&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#ords&quot;&gt;Customer Managed Oracle REST Data Services&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#wmph&quot;&gt;Workload metrics on performance Hub&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#tzs&quot;&gt;Timezone selector on Perf Hub&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#nlm&quot;&gt;Latency metrics now available&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#tdv&quot;&gt;Easy access to tenancy details&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#nvc&quot;&gt;New ADB collateral&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#dwgl&quot;&gt;Global Leaders Update&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
						&lt;/ul&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;Don&amp;#39;t forget to checkout our &lt;strong&gt;&amp;quot;What&amp;#39;s New&amp;quot;&lt;/strong&gt; page for a comprehensive archive of all the new features we have added to Autonomous Database - &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.oracle.com/database/technologies/datawarehouse-bigdata/adw-features.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;To find out how to subscribe to this newsletter &lt;a href=&quot;https://blogs.oracle.com/datawarehousing/announcing-customer-newsletter-for-autonomous-database&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			
			&lt;a name=&quot;ords&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Icon for Oracle REST Data Services&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/7c314c5eb281bdacd2d13ed4f5ea6513/ords_icon.png&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - ADB now supports Customer Managed Oracle REST Data Services&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;When you use the default ORDS on Autonomous Database, you cannot modify any of the ORDS configuration options. For example, with the default configuration connections for ORDS are preconfigured to use the LOW database service.&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						You can now use a customer managed environment if you want manual control of the configuration and management of Oracle REST Data Services.&lt;/p&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Workload Metrics on Performance Hub&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;Performance Hub has been expanded to include a new tab, &amp;quot;Workload&amp;quot;. This can be used to monitor the workload in the database and helps the user identify performance spikes and bottlenecks.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;There are 4 regions in this tab: CPU Statistics, Wait Time Statistics, Workload Profile, and Sessions. Each region contains a group of charts that indicate the characteristics of the workload and the distribution of the resources, as shown below.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;img alt=&quot;Autonomous Database Performance Hub console showing new workload metrics&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/4a8e4a66f3bb40e0acc33f54110273f8/perf_hub_workload_500.jpg&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;IMAGE - view the screenshot of the new Workload tab containing the four regions and their associated charts are displayed - &lt;a href=&quot;https://einstein.oracle.com/a/yIpElJgQ-8416-mMxVbjPb&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Performance Hub Now Has a Timezone Selector&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;A time zone control has been added to Performance Hub. This will allow users to view data using an alternate time zone to UTC. They will have the choice of viewing data using either UTC (default), the time zone of their browser client, or the time zone of the database.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;

						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;ADB provides extensions for key IDEs to support common operations&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/0fc248c4f754c74fa282aa6b7bc21c71/ic_developer_female_gray.gif&quot; /&gt;

						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Latency Metrics Now Available in Service Metrics&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;The Database Service Metrics information help Cloud Admins measure useful quantitative data about their Autonomous Databases. This list of available metrics now includes two new latency metrics:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:25px&quot;&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;1) Connection latency - Time taken (in milliseconds) to connect to an Autonomous Database that uses shared Exadata infrastructure in each region from a Compute service virtual machine in the same region.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;2) Query latency/response time - Time taken (in milliseconds) to display the results of a simple query on the user&amp;#39;s screen.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Note - the tests to measure connection latency and query latency are not run against any customer instances.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;Within the Service Metrics console, it is possible to define and publish alarms against these new metrics.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;img alt=&quot;Service Metrics OCI console showing new latency metrics&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/4a8e4a66f3bb40e0acc33f54110273f8/perf_hub_workload_500.jpg&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;IMAGE - view the screenshot of the new latency metrics graphs on Service Metrics console- &lt;a href=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/e890af1af70c746c2d2cd950bfee48a5/latency_metrics_800.png&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - SQL access to tenancy details for ADB&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;When you file a service request for Autonomous Database, you need to provide the tenancy details for your instance. Tenancy details for the instance are available on the Oracle Cloud Infrastructure console. However, if you are connected to the database, you can now obtain these details by querying the &lt;strong&gt;CLOUD_IDENTITY&lt;/strong&gt; column of the &lt;strong&gt;V$PDBS view&lt;/strong&gt;. For example:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot; style=&quot;font-family:courier !important; margin-left:40px;&quot;&gt;SELECT cloud_identity&lt;br /&gt;
						FROM v$pdbs;&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;...will generate something similar to the following:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot; style=&quot;font-family:courier !important; margin-left:40px;&quot;&gt;{&amp;quot;DATABASE_NAME&amp;quot; : &amp;quot;DBxxxxxxxxxxxx&amp;quot;,&lt;br /&gt;
						&amp;quot;REGION&amp;quot; : &amp;quot;us-phoenix-1&amp;quot;,&lt;br /&gt;
						&amp;quot;TENANT_OCID&amp;quot; : &amp;quot;OCID1.TENANCY.REGION1..ID1&amp;quot;,&lt;br /&gt;
						&amp;quot;DATABASE_OCID&amp;quot; : &amp;quot;OCID1.AUTONOMOUSDATABASE.OC1.SEA.ID2&amp;quot;,&lt;br /&gt;
						&amp;quot;COMPARTMENT_OCID&amp;quot; : &amp;quot;ocid1.tenancy.region1..ID3&amp;quot;}&lt;/p&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

						
							
								
									LEARN MORE

						&amp;nbsp;
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:20px; margin-right:20px; background-color: rgba(128,128,128, 0.8); color: white;text-align: left; font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; height:170px; font-weight:bold;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;margin-left:20px; font-size:25pt; line-height:1.5;&quot;&gt;Autonomous Database&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;margin-left:20px; font-size:15pt; line-height:1.5;&quot;&gt;on Shared Exadata Infrastructure&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;margin-left:20px; font-size:12pt; line-height:1.5;&quot;&gt;April 30, 2020&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;
						&lt;img alt=&quot;ADB Logo&quot; class=&quot;header_icon&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/3171ecca19062436f699f9aedcd05812/adb_header_icon_300.jpeg&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:20px;&quot; /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			
			&lt;a name=&quot;btt&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:20px;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;
						&lt;p&gt;Welcome to our latest customer newsletter for Autonomous Database on Shared Exadata Infrastructure.&amp;nbsp;This newsletter covers the following new features and topics:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;ul&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#sla&quot;&gt;Service Level Agreement for ADB&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#psb&quot;&gt;Per-second billing&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#soda&quot;&gt;Support for SODA documents and collections&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#side&quot;&gt;ADB Extensions for IDEs&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#srs&quot;&gt;Stateful Rule Support in Private Endpoints&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#dpe&quot;&gt;Enhancements for Data Pump&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#dwgl&quot;&gt;Global Leaders Program - Update&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#qle&quot;&gt;Quick Links&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
						&lt;/ul&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;Don&amp;#39;t forget to checkout our &lt;strong&gt;&amp;quot;What&amp;#39;s New&amp;quot;&lt;/strong&gt; page for a comprehensive archive of all the new features we have added to Autonomous Database - &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.oracle.com/database/technologies/datawarehouse-bigdata/adw-features.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;To find out how to subscribe to this newsletter &lt;a href=&quot;https://blogs.oracle.com/datawarehousing/announcing-customer-newsletter-for-autonomous-database&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			
			&lt;a name=&quot;sla&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Icon for Oracle PaaS and IaaS Public Cloud Services Pillar Document&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://keithlaker.github.io/Publishing/doc-yellow.png&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Autonomous Database now comes with an SLA&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;The service level agreement for ADB has just been published and it applies only to the deployment of an Autonomous Database on shared infrastructure.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;The pillar document listed below in the section headed &lt;strong&gt;LEARN&lt;/strong&gt; states that:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot; style=&quot;margin-left:30px; margin-right:50px;&quot;&gt;&lt;em&gt;Oracle will use commercially reasonable efforts to have the Oracle Cloud Infrastructure &amp;ndash; Autonomous Database Services on Shared Infrastructure with a Monthly Uptime Percentage of at least 99.95% during any calendar month (the &amp;quot;Service Commitment&amp;quot;). &lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;In the event an Autonomous Database Service on Shared Infrastructure does not meet the &amp;quot;Service Commitment&amp;quot; then customers will be eligible to receive Service Credits. Note - there are specific definitions of key terms in the pillar document (&lt;em&gt;listed below in the section headed &lt;strong&gt;LEARN&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/em&gt;) that you should read and understand.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;
						
							
								
									LEARN MORE
								
							
						

						
							
								
									
									&lt;div class=&quot;row_set&quot;&gt;
									&lt;p&gt;PDF: Oracle PaaS and IaaS Public Cloud Services Pillar Document (April 2020),&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://www.oracle.com/assets/paas-iaas-pub-cld-srvs-pillar-4021422.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;Autonomous Database information is covered in Category 7, which starts on page 4 with ADB covered on pages 17 and 18.&lt;/p&gt;
									&lt;/div&gt;
									
								
							
						
						
						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			

			
				
					
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;a class=&quot;btt&quot; href=&quot;#btt&quot;&gt;BACK TO TOP&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			
			&lt;a name=&quot;psb&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Icon showing per second billing for Autonomous Database&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/7262f9add7a1acfa96751223c00098ab/psb.png&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Per-Second Billing For Autonomous Database&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;Autonomous Database instance CPU and storage usage is now billed by the second, with a minimum usage period of one minute. Previously Autonomous Database billed in one-hour minimum increments and partial usage of an hour was rounded up to a full hour.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;This change benefits the following types of use cases:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;ul&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Where you only run your ADB instances during work hours and stop instances at end of working day&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Where you start-stop your instances to run overnight batch jobs&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Where you have ADB instances which typically have a short lifecycle &amp;ndash; sandboxes, QA, training, integration testing instances.&lt;/li&gt;
						&lt;/ul&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

						
							
								
									LEARN MORE
								
							
						

						
							
								
									
									&lt;div class=&quot;row_set&quot;&gt;
									&lt;p&gt;DOC: Per-second billing announcement for ADW,&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class=&quot;doc&quot; href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/autonomous-data-warehouse-cloud/whats-new/index.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;DOC: Per-second billing announcement for ATP,&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class=&quot;doc&quot; href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/atp-cloud/atpwn/index.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;DOC: OCI Per-second billing general announcement which covers ADB,&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class=&quot;doc&quot; href=&quot;https://docs.cloud.oracle.com/en-us/iaas/Content/Database/Concepts/adboverview.htm#persecondbilling&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;BLOG: Review of per-second billing on OCI,&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class=&quot;doc&quot; href=&quot;https://blogs.oracle.com/cloud-infrastructure/announcing-per-second-billing-for-compute-and-autonomous-database&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
									&lt;/div&gt;
									
								
							
						
						
						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			

			
				
					
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;a class=&quot;btt&quot; href=&quot;#btt&quot;&gt;BACK TO TOP&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			
			&lt;a name=&quot;soda&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Autonomous Database offers extended support for SODA documents and collections&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/74c05585d162d8b066f67e5710f40956/soda.png&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Support for SODA Documents and Collections&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;
						&lt;p&gt;Autonomous Database now supports loading and using Simple Oracle Document Architecture (SODA) documents and collections. SODA allows developers to store, search, and retrieve document collections, typically JSON documents, without using SQL.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;It is possible to also access document collections with SQL/JSON operators which means that ADB now combines the simplicity of a &lt;em&gt;document database&lt;/em&gt; with the power of a relational database.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;The Oracle Cloud Infrastructure console has been updated with a link to access the SODA drivers for several languages and frameworks including: Java, Node.js, Python, Oracle Call Interface, and PL/SQL, as shown below.&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;img alt=&quot;Autonomous Database tools panel on OCI console showing access to new SODA drivers&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/9a8055c01a2f6125879db44402e21dcf/tools_soda_500.png&quot; /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;
						
							
								
									LEARN MORE
								
							
						

						
							
								
									
									&lt;div class=&quot;row_set&quot;&gt;
									&lt;p&gt;DOC: Using JSON Documents with ADW,&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class=&quot;doc&quot; href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/autonomous-data-warehouse-cloud/user/document-database.html#GUID-78AA9D61-7370-44D3-BB58-D236FEB19CFB&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;DOC: Using JSON Documents with ATP,&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class=&quot;doc&quot; href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/atp-cloud/atpug/document-database.html#GUID-78AA9D61-7370-44D3-BB58-D236FEB19CFB&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;Documentation covers the following key topics:&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;ul&gt;
										&lt;li&gt;Work with Simple Oracle Document Access (SODA) in Autonomous Database&lt;/li&gt;
										&lt;li&gt;SODA Collection Metadata on Autonomous Database&lt;/li&gt;
										&lt;li&gt;Work with JSON Documents Using SQL and PL/SQL APIs on Autonomous Database&lt;/li&gt;
										&lt;li&gt;Load JSON Documents with Autonomous Database&lt;/li&gt;
									&lt;/ul&gt;
									&lt;/div&gt;
									
								
							
						

						&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;

						
							
								
									DO MORE
								
							
						

						
							
								
									
									&lt;div class=&quot;row_set&quot;&gt;
									&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;For examples of using SODA see the following whitepaper:&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class=&quot;doc&quot; href=&quot;https://www.oracle.com/technetwork/database/appdev-with-soda-2606220.pdf&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Developing schemaless applications using the Simple Oracle Document Access APIs&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
									&lt;br /&gt;
									&amp;nbsp;&lt;/div&gt;
									
								
							
						
						
						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			

			
				
					
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;a class=&quot;btt&quot; href=&quot;#btt&quot;&gt;BACK TO TOP&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			
			&lt;a name=&quot;side&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;ADB provides extensions for key IDEs to support common operations&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/0fc248c4f754c74fa282aa6b7bc21c71/ic_developer_female_gray.gif&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - ADB Extensions for IDEs&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;ADB extensions enable developers to connect to, browse, and manage Autonomous Databases directly from their IDEs. There are extensions for the following: Eclipse, Microsoft Visual Studio and Visual Studio Code.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;Users with permissions to manage the databases can perform a number of actions (&lt;em&gt;depending on their IDE&lt;/em&gt;), such as:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;ul&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Sign up for Oracle Cloud&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Connect to a cloud account using a simple auto-generated config file and key file&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Create new or clone existing Always Free Autonomous Database, Autonomous Database Dedicated, and Autonomous Database Shared databases&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Automatically download credentials files (including wallets) and quickly connect, browse, and operate on Autonomous Database schemas&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Change compartments and regions without reconnecting&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Start, stop, or terminate Autonomous Databases&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Scale up/down Autonomous Database resources&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Restore from backup&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Update instance credentials and/or license type used&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Rotate wallets&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Convert Always Free ADBs into paid ADBs&lt;/li&gt;
						&lt;/ul&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

						
							
								
									LEARN MORE
								
							
						

						
							
								
									
									&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:300px; margin-right:100px; color:white !important;&quot;&gt;
									&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;DOC: IDE Extensions in ADW,&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class=&quot;doc&quot; href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/autonomous-data-warehouse-cloud/user/develop-with-ide-extensions.html#GUID-35F30F17-26D6-4897-A587-6AB14BB5B68A&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;DOC: IDE Extensions in ATP,&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class=&quot;doc&quot; href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/atp-cloud/atpug/develop-with-ide-extensions.html#GUID-35F30F17-26D6-4897-A587-6AB14BB5B68A&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
									&lt;/div&gt;
									
								
							
						
						
						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			

			
				
					
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;a class=&quot;btt&quot; href=&quot;#btt&quot;&gt;BACK TO TOP&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			
			&lt;a name=&quot;srs&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Feature Icon&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://www.oracle.com/ocom/groups/public/@otn/documents/digitalasset/3449984.png&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Stateful Rule Support in Private Endpoints&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;When configuring a private endpoint one of the steps is to define a security rule(s) in a Network Security Group. This creates a virtual firewall for the Autonomous Database and allows connections to the Autonomous Database instance.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;The Network Security Group can now be configured with stateful rules.&lt;/p&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

						
							
								
									LEARN MORE
								
							
						

						
							
								
									
									&lt;div class=&quot;row_set&quot;&gt;
									&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;DOC: Configure Private Endpoints with ADW, &lt;a class=&quot;doc&quot; href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/autonomous-data-warehouse-cloud/user/access-private-endpoint.html#GUID-2D6A7F84-C7F1-4149-867B-12106F1F7E66&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;DOC: Configure Private Endpoints with ATP, &lt;a class=&quot;doc&quot; href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/atp-cloud/atpug/access-private-endpoint.html#GUID-2D6A7F84-C7F1-4149-867B-12106F1F7E66&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

									&lt;p&gt;BLOG: Announcing Private Endpoints in Autonomous Database on Shared Exadata Infrastructure, &lt;a class=&quot;doc&quot; href=&quot;https://blogs.oracle.com/datawarehousing/announcing-private-endpoints-in-autonomous-database-on-shared-exadata-infrastructure-v2&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
									&lt;/div&gt;

			&lt;a name=&quot;dpe&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Enhancements to How Autonomous Database Can Leverage Data Pump Dump Files&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/d75f752a236eb0545a8f48d18f202313/gsm_logo1_3664622.png&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;UPDATED &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Enhancements to Data Pump Support&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;Two specific improvements relating to how Data Pump dump files can be used with ADB. It is now possible to:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;ul&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Query Data Pump dump files in the Cloud by creating an external table&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;Use Data Pump dump files in the Cloud as source files to load data&lt;/li&gt;
						&lt;/ul&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

									&amp;nbsp;

			&lt;a name=&quot;btt&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:20px;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;
						&lt;p&gt;Welcome to our latest customer newsletter for Autonomous Database on Shared Exadata Infrastructure.&amp;nbsp;This newsletter covers the following new features and topics:&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;Don&amp;#39;t forget to checkout our &lt;strong&gt;&amp;quot;What&amp;#39;s New&amp;quot;&lt;/strong&gt; page for a comprehensive archive of all the new features we have added to Autonomous Database - &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.oracle.com/database/technologies/datawarehouse-bigdata/adw-features.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;ul&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#db19&quot;&gt;Options for upgrading to Database 19c&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#odpe&quot;&gt;Enhancements to Data Pump&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#ocir&quot;&gt;New menu option to restart ADB instances&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#wrmf&quot;&gt;Enhacements to wallets&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#dwgl&quot;&gt;Global Leaders Program - Update&lt;/a&gt;
							&lt;ul&gt;
								&lt;li&gt;Day-with-Development Program&lt;/li&gt;

						&amp;nbsp;
					
				
			
			&lt;a name=&quot;db19&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

			
				
					
						
						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Feature Icon&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/7452caec8faf22b604482d875395e694/19c_logo.png&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
						
						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Upgrade an Autonomous Database Instance to Oracle Database 19c&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;Oracle Database 19c is now available on Autonomous Database for all regions. In select regions, customers can choose between Oracle Database 18c and Oracle Database 19c for new databases. The default version for all new databases is 19c and going forward, most new Autonomous Database features will only be available for databases using Oracle Database 19c.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;Please start planning for the upgrade of your applications to Database 19c. For most applications, there should not be any changes required. However, it is recommended you should test your applications with Database 19c. You can easily test your applications by creating a clone of your current database to Oracle Database 19c, and testing your application using this clone.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;Oracle Database 18c is scheduled to be available in Autonomous Database until September 2020.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;You can choose to upgrade your database at any time during this period. After that time, all existing databases will be automatically upgraded to Oracle Database 19c. There are several approaches to upgrading your database which are described in the documentation, see links below.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note:&lt;/strong&gt; Autonomous Database plans to offer a new upgrade path starting in April, with a single button that provides a one-way, in-place upgrade.&lt;/p&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

						&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt;1) Support For Pre-Authenticated URLs&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;This enhancement allows Oracle Data Pump to use Oracle Cloud Infrastructure pre-authenticated URIs for source files on Oracle Cloud Infrastructure Object Storage.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;: Customers should carefully assess the business requirement for and the security ramifications of pre-authenticated access. There is more guidance available in the documentation.&lt;/p&gt;

This simplifies the process of moving data between Autonomous Data Warehouse and other Oracle databases. This export method is supported with Oracle Cloud Infrastructure Object Storage and Oracle Cloud Infrastructure Object Storage Classic.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:20px;&quot;&gt;
							&lt;br&gt;
							&lt;p&gt;Welcome to our latest customer newsletter for Autonomous Database on Shared Exadata Infrastructure.&amp;nbsp;This newsletter covers the following new features and topics:
							&lt;/p&gt;
							&lt;ol&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#dbve&quot;&gt;Support for Private Endpoints&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#dwgl&quot;&gt;Global Leaders Program - Update&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
								&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#qle&quot;&gt;Quick Links&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;/ol&gt;
							&lt;p&gt;Don&amp;#39;t forget to checkout our &lt;strong&gt;&amp;quot;What&amp;#39;s New&amp;quot;&lt;/strong&gt; page for a comprehensive archive of all the new features we have added to Autonomous Database - &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.oracle.com/database/technologies/datawarehouse-bigdata/adw-features.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.
							&lt;/p&gt;
							&lt;br&gt;
						&lt;/div&gt;
					
					
					
				
			
			&lt;a name=&quot;dbve&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
			
				
					
						
							&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;
								&lt;img alt=&quot;Feature Icon&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://www.oracle.com/ocom/groups/public/@otn/documents/digitalasset/3449984.png&quot; /&gt;
								&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
									Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
									Only)
								&lt;/p&gt;
							&lt;/div&gt;
						
						
							&lt;br&gt;
							&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Autonomous Database Now Supports Private Endpoints&lt;/span&gt;
							&lt;p&gt;
								It is now possible to restrict access to Autonomous Database by specifying a private endpoint within a Virtual Cloud Network (VCN). Configuration of private access is done when provisioning or cloning an Autonomous Database - allowing all traffic to and from an Autonomous Database to be kept off the public internet.
							&lt;/p&gt;
							&lt;p&gt;
								During provisioning or cloning, it is possible to specify private access for an Autonomous Database by selecting &lt;strong&gt;Virtual cloud network&lt;/strong&gt; within the &lt;strong&gt;Choose network access&lt;/strong&gt; section of the create/clone dialog, as shown below:
							&lt;/p&gt;
							&lt;br&gt;
							&lt;img moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; class=&quot;header_icon&quot; width=&quot;550px&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/1e721cf94944136be6021057e7a6b934/adb_private_vcn.png&quot; alt=&quot;ADB Logo&quot;&gt;
							&lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/autonomous-data-warehouse-cloud/user/img_text/adb_private_vcn.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Description of the illustration adb_private_vcn.png&lt;/a&gt;
							&lt;/p&gt;
							&lt;br&gt;
							&lt;p&gt;
								The configuration process for enablishing private endpoints involves three steps which must be done before provisioning or cloning an Autonomous Database:
							&lt;/p&gt;
							&lt;ol&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt;Create a VCN within the region that will contain your Autonomous Database.
								&lt;/li&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt;Configure a subnet within the VCN, configured with default DHCP options.
								&lt;/li&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt;Specify at least one network security group (NSG) within the VCN - &lt;em&gt;used to specify the ingress and egress rules for the Autonomous Database&lt;/em&gt;.
								&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;/ol&gt;
							&lt;p&gt;
								&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;Note&lt;/span&gt;: Private Endpoints is currently rolling out across all ou data centers. As of today, Feb 26, it is live in the following data centers:
							&lt;/p&gt;
							&lt;ul&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt; Amsterdam&lt;/li&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt; Ashburn&lt;/li&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt; Frankfurt&lt;/li&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt; Jeddah&lt;/li&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt; London&lt;/li&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt; Melbourne&lt;/li&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt; Osaka&lt;/li&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt; Phoenix&lt;/li&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt; Seoul&lt;/li&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt; Tokyo&lt;/li&gt;
								&lt;li class=&quot;scl-facebook&quot;&gt; Toronto&lt;/li&gt;
							&lt;/ul&gt;
							&lt;p&gt;
								It will be available shortly in the remaining data centers.
							&lt;/p&gt;
							&lt;br&gt;
							&lt;br&gt;

							&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;EVENTS &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; Oracle Global Leaders - Day With Development&lt;/span&gt;

						&lt;div style=&quot;margin-left:10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Feature Icon&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://www.oracle.com/ocom/groups/public/@otn/documents/digitalasset/3449984.png&quot; /&gt;

						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Using Oracle Database Vault with Autonomous Database&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;Oracle Database Vault implements powerful security controls for your Autonomous Database. These unique security controls restrict access to application data by privileged database users, reducing the risk of insider and outside threats and addressing common compliance requirements.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Always Free Autonomous Database now includes APEX 19.2&lt;/span&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;Oracle APEX 19.2 on Always Free Autonomous Database provides a preconfigured, fully managed and secured environment to both build and deploy world-class data-centric applications. Oracle APEX applications developed on-premise can be easily deployed to Oracle APEX on the free version Autonomous Database.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Multiple Database Versions and Availability by Region&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;Depending on the region where you provision or clone your database, Autonomous Database now supports one or more Oracle Database versions. The version availability depends on the region - note that some regions do not support multiple Oracle Database versions.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;When multiple database versions are available, you choose an Oracle Database version when you provision or clone a database&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;img alt=&quot;Feature Icon&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/5c89b98bfa53e7c0d4fe74e99f71f7dd/graph_icon.png&quot; /&gt;

						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;

						&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Availability of Oracle Graph Server and Client 20.1&lt;/span&gt;
						&lt;p&gt;Oracle Graph Server and Client 20.1 is a software package that works with Autonomous Database. It includes the in-memory analytics server (PGX) and client libraries required to work with the Property Graph feature in Autonomous Database.&lt;/p&gt;

						&lt;p&gt;With graph analytics you can explore and discover connections and patterns in social networks, IoT, big data, data warehouses, and complex transaction data for applications such as fraud detection in banking, customer 360, and smart manufacturing.&lt;/p&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

						&lt;img alt=&quot;Feature Icon&quot; moz-do-not-send=&quot;true&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/b0e0d4b2c6c6a0631d4124dfe83331a0/db_icon.jpg&quot; /&gt;
						&lt;p class=&quot;serverless&quot;&gt;(Shared&lt;br /&gt;
						Infrastructure&lt;br /&gt;
						Only)&lt;/p&gt;
						
						
						&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;
						&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight:bold; color:red;&quot;&gt;NEW &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;feature_header&quot;&gt; - Features to Simplify Migrations To ADB&lt;/span&gt;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;1. Database Resident Connection Pool (DRCP)&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						Using DRCP provides you with access to a connection pool in your ADB that enables a significant reduction in key database resources required to support many client connections. See Use Database Resident Connection Pooling with Autonomous Database for more information.&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						DOC: ADW &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.oracle.com/pls/topic/lookup?ctx=en/cloud/paas/autonomous-data-warehouse-cloud/whats-new&amp;amp;id=CSWHU-GUID-E1337EC6-4A78-4199-84F0-A2739055F3FA&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;br /&gt;
						DOC: ATP &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/atp-cloud/atpug/connect-drcp.html#GUID-E1337EC6-4A78-4199-84F0-A2739055F3FA&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;2. Set MAX_STRING_SIZE value&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						By default the Autonomous Data Warehouse database uses MAX_STRING_SIZE set to the value EXTENDED. To support migration from older Oracle Databases or applications you can set MAX_STRING_SIZE to the value STANDARD. See Checking and Setting MAX_STRING_SIZE for more information.&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						DOC: ADW &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/autonomous-data-warehouse-cloud/user/experienced-database-users.html#GUID-7340C837-FD5F-489D-9348-A4E86846323F&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;br /&gt;
						DOC: ATP &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/atp-cloud/atpug/experienced-database-users.html#GUID-7340C837-FD5F-489D-9348-A4E86846323F&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
						&amp;nbsp;

						&lt;p class=&quot;basic_text&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;3. Number of concurrent statements&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
						The maximum number of concurrent statements is increased. See Predefined Database Service Names for Autonomous Data Warehouse for more information.&lt;br /&gt;
						&lt;br /&gt;
						DOC: ADW &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/autonomous-data-warehouse-cloud/user/connect-predefined.html#GUID-9747539B-FD46-44F1-8FF8-F5AC650F15BE&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;br /&gt;
						DOC: ATP &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.oracle.com/en/cloud/paas/atp-cloud/atpug/connect-predefined.html#GUID-9747539B-FD46-44F1-8FF8-F5AC650F15BE&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

            <title>Announcing Our New Customer Newsletter for Autonomous Database - Don't Miss Out!</title>
            <link>https://blogs.oracle.com/datawarehousing/announcing-our-new-customer-newsletter-for-autonomous-database-dont-miss-out</link>
            <description>Welcome

&lt;p&gt;I am happy to announce that I will be posting a regular customer newsletter&amp;nbsp;for Autonomous Database (&lt;em&gt;on Shared Exadata Infrastructure&lt;/em&gt;) on this blog. It will cover the latest features added to&amp;nbsp;Autonomous Database with links to additional collateral such as specific doc pages, videos, whitepapers, etc. Typically we are delivering new features every 3-4 weeks so this newsletter will appear on a regular basis throughout the year.&lt;/p&gt;

How Do I Subscribe?

&lt;p&gt;If you want to subscribe to an RSS feed that will automatically refresh when each newsletter is posted then here are the steps...&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;1) Goto &lt;a href=&quot;https://blogs.oracle.com/datawarehousing/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;blogs.oracle.com/datawarehousing&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;2) Click on the three horizontal lines next to a magnifying glass&amp;nbsp;in the top-right corner of the page to open the menu showing the list of categories for this blog&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/56910eb3fc7caf2dc21eda41fe8883eb/screen_shot_2020_02_18_at_11_35_41.png&quot; style=&quot;width: 178px; height: 122px;&quot; /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;3) Now select the category &amp;quot;&lt;em&gt;Newsletter&lt;/em&gt;&amp;quot;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/4337e7826d9a5edc81e7f21fe53988ef/screen_shot_2020_02_18_at_11_37_47.png&quot; /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;This will take you to the following page...&lt;a href=&quot;https://blogs.oracle.com/datawarehousing/newsletter&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;https://blogs.oracle.com/datawarehousing/newsletter&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;(&lt;em&gt;yes, you are quite correct - I could have simply given you this link at the top of the page but this way you get to view the different categories available on the data warehouse blog so you can easily register for other areas&lt;/em&gt;).&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;4) Now click on the last icon on the right in the group of four...this is the RSS feed icon&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/576587a8d349b8ed2c70b2e59c6625a4/screen_shot_2020_02_18_at_11_38_47.png&quot; style=&quot;width: 240px; height: 92px;&quot; /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;5) If you just want the RSS feed to include the newsletters then select the second option &amp;quot;Only This Category&amp;#39;s Posts&amp;quot;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;&quot; src=&quot;https://cdn.app.compendium.com/uploads/user/e7c690e8-6ff9-102a-ac6d-e4aebca50425/3f1f9085-e459-4b23-85f7-ed09e21ffb29/Image/b07b906a01d510effac30938626bfe77/screen_shot_2020_02_18_at_11_41_48.png&quot; style=&quot;width: 290px; height: 160px;&quot; /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;All done! You will probably get a pop-up to authorise access to your local application for viewing RSS feeds.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;

When Is The First Edition

&lt;p&gt;The first edition will be out very soon! Yes, it&amp;#39;s free.&amp;nbsp;Hope you enjoy our newsletter.&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;
</description>
